﻿// Services/UserProfile/Interface/IUserProfileService.cs
using ThriftLoop.DTOs.User;
using ThriftLoop.Enums;

namespace ThriftLoop.Services.UserProfile.Interface;

public interface IUserProfileService
{
    /// <summary>
    /// Returns a read-only profile snapshot for the given user ID.
    /// Returns null when the user does not exist.
    /// </summary>
    Task<UserProfileDTO?> GetProfileAsync(int userId);

    /// <summary>
    /// Applies FullName, PhoneNumber, and Address from the DTO.
    /// Returns false when the user does not exist.
    /// </summary>
    Task<bool> UpdateProfileAsync(int userId, UpdateProfileDTO dto);

    // ─────────────────────────────────────────
    //  SELLER APPLICATION
    // ─────────────────────────────────────────

    /// <summary>
    /// Returns the user's current seller application, or null if they have
    /// never submitted one.
    /// </summary>
    Task<SellerApplicationStatusDTO?> GetSellerApplicationAsync(int userId);

    /// <summary>
    /// Creates a new seller application for the given user.
    /// Saves the gov-ID file under <paramref name="uploadsRootPath"/>/gov-ids/.
    /// </summary>
    /// <param name="userId">The authenticated user's ID.</param>
    /// <param name="dto">Form data including the uploaded gov-ID file.</param>
    /// <param name="uploadsRootPath">
    ///   Absolute path to the wwwroot/uploads directory, typically
    ///   Path.Combine(env.WebRootPath, "uploads").
    /// </param>
    /// <returns>
    ///   <see cref="SellerApplicationResult.Success"/> on success;
    ///   one of the other values if the request cannot be fulfilled.
    /// </returns>
    Task<SellerApplicationResult> SubmitSellerApplicationAsync(
        int userId,
        SellerApplicationDTO dto,
        string uploadsRootPath);
}

--- Services\Interface\IWalletService.cs ---
﻿using ThriftLoop.Enums;
using ThriftLoop.Models;

namespace ThriftLoop.Services.WalletManagement.Interface;

public interface IWalletService
{
    /// <summary>
    /// Returns the wallet for <paramref name="userId"/> (dbo.Users), creating
    /// and seeding it with a demo balance if one does not yet exist.
    /// </summary>
    Task<Wallet> GetOrCreateWalletAsync(int userId);

    /// <summary>
    /// Returns the wallet for <paramref name="riderId"/> (dbo.Riders), creating
    /// it with a zero balance if one does not yet exist.
    /// Riders and Users are separate tables — this sets Wallet.RiderId, not UserId.
    /// </summary>
    Task<Wallet> GetOrCreateRiderWalletAsync(int riderId);

    /// <summary>
    /// Moves <paramref name="amount"/> from the buyer's available Balance into
    /// their PendingBalance (escrow hold). The full amount includes the item
    /// price and the flat delivery fee.
    /// Returns <c>false</c> if the buyer has insufficient funds.
    /// </summary>
    Task<bool> HoldEscrowAsync(int orderId, int buyerId, decimal amount);

    /// <summary>
    /// Releases the item-price portion of the escrow to the seller.
    /// Pass <c>amount = order.FinalPrice − order.DeliveryFee</c>.
    /// The delivery-fee slice is released separately via
    /// <see cref="PayRiderAsync"/> with <c>fromEscrow = true</c>.
    /// </summary>
    Task ReleaseEscrowAsync(int orderId, int buyerId, int sellerId, decimal amount);

    /// <summary>
    /// Records a cash-on-delivery payment to the seller's wallet.
    /// Pass <c>amount = order.FinalPrice − order.DeliveryFee</c> (item price only).
    /// The delivery fee is credited to the rider separately via
    /// <see cref="PayRiderAsync"/> with <c>fromEscrow = false</c>.
    /// </summary>
    Task RecordCashCollectionAsync(int orderId, int buyerId, int sellerId, decimal amount);

    /// <summary>
    /// Credits the flat delivery fee to the rider's wallet after a successful delivery.
    /// <paramref name="riderId"/> is a Riders.Id — NOT a Users.Id.
    ///
    /// <paramref name="fromEscrow"/> = <c>true</c>  (Wallet orders):
    ///   Also debits the buyer's PendingBalance by <paramref name="deliveryFee"/>.
    ///   Call after <see cref="ReleaseEscrowAsync"/> to fully drain the escrow.
    ///
    /// <paramref name="fromEscrow"/> = <c>false</c> (COD orders):
    ///   The buyer already paid in cash. Only the rider's Balance is updated.
    /// </summary>
    Task PayRiderAsync(
        int orderId,
        int buyerId,
        int riderId,
        decimal deliveryFee,
        bool fromEscrow = false);

    /// <summary>Adds <paramref name="amount"/> to the user's available Balance.</summary>
    Task TopUpAsync(int userId, decimal amount);

    /// <summary>
    /// Debits <paramref name="amount"/> from the user's Balance and creates a
    /// Withdrawal record with <see cref="WithdrawalStatus.Requested"/>.
    /// Returns <c>false</c> if the balance is insufficient.
    /// </summary>
    Task<bool> RequestWithdrawalAsync(
        int userId, decimal amount, WithdrawalMethod method, string? reference);

    /// <summary>
    /// Transfers <paramref name="amount"/> directly from buyer's available Balance
    /// to seller's Balance (wallet-to-wallet payment without escrow).
    /// Throws <see cref="InvalidOperationException"/> if buyer has insufficient funds.
    /// </summary>
    Task TransferWalletToWalletAsync(int orderId, int buyerId, int sellerId, decimal amount);
}

﻿// ViewModels/Admin/AdminDashboardViewModel.cs
using ThriftLoop.Models;
using ThriftLoop.Enums;

namespace ThriftLoop.ViewModels.Admin;

public class AdminDashboardViewModel
{
    // ── Statistics Cards ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    public int TotalUsers { get; set; }
    public int TotalSellers { get; set; }
    public int TotalRiders { get; set; }
    public int TotalOrders { get; set; }
    public decimal TotalRevenue { get; set; }
    public decimal PendingWithdrawals { get; set; }
    public int PendingSellerApprovals { get; set; }
    public int PendingRiderApprovals { get; set; }

    // ── Recent Activity Lists ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
    public IReadOnlyList<User> RecentUsers { get; set; } = new List<User>();
    public IReadOnlyList<Withdrawal> RecentWithdrawals { get; set; } = new List<Withdrawal>();
    public IReadOnlyList<SellerProfile> RecentSellerApplications { get; set; } = new List<SellerProfile>();
    public IReadOnlyList<Rider> RecentRiderApplications { get; set; } = new List<Rider>();

    // ── Computed Properties ───────────────────────────────────────────────────
    public decimal TotalPlatformValue => TotalRevenue + PendingWithdrawals;
}

--- ViewModels\Admin\UserManagementViewModel.cs ---
﻿// ViewModels/Admin/UserManagementViewModel.cs
using ThriftLoop.Models;
using ThriftLoop.Enums;

namespace ThriftLoop.ViewModels.Admin;

public class UserManagementViewModel
{
    // ── User List ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    public IReadOnlyList<User> Users { get; set; } = new List<User>();

    // ─── Filtering & Pagination ───────────────────────────────────────────────
    public string? SearchTerm { get; set; }
    public string? RoleFilter { get; set; }
    public int CurrentPage { get; set; }
    public int TotalPages { get; set; }
    public int TotalCount { get; set; }

    // ── Available Filters (for dropdowns) ─────────────────────────────────────
    public static IReadOnlyList<string> RoleFilters => new[]
    {
        "All",
        nameof(UserRole.User),
        nameof(UserRole.Seller),
        nameof(UserRole.Admin)
    };

    // ── Computed Properties ───────────────────────────────────────────────────
    public bool HasPreviousPage => CurrentPage > 1;
    public bool HasNextPage => CurrentPage < TotalPages;

    public string GetRoleBadgeClass(UserRole role)
    {
        return role switch
        {
            UserRole.Admin => "badge-admin",
            UserRole.Seller => "badge-seller",
            UserRole.User => "badge-user",
            UserRole.Rider => "badge-rider",
            _ => "badge-default"
        };
    }

    public string GetStatusBadgeClass(bool isDisabled)
    {
        return isDisabled ? "badge-disabled" : "badge-active";
    }

    public string GetStatusText(bool isDisabled)
    {
        return isDisabled ? "Disabled" : "Active";
    }
}

@section Scripts {
    <script>
        (function() {
            const fileInput = document.getElementById('qrImage');
            const previewContainer = document.getElementById('previewContainer');
            const previewImage = document.getElementById('previewImage');

            if (fileInput) {
                fileInput.addEventListener('change', function() {
                    const file = this.files[0];
                    if (file) {
                        const reader = new FileReader();
                        reader.onload = function(e) {
                            previewImage.src = e.target.result;
                            previewContainer.style.display = 'block';
                        };
                        reader.readAsDataURL(file);
                    }
                });
            }
        })();
        
        function clearAccountNumber() {
            if (confirm('Clear the GCash account number? Transactions will no longer be validated against a specific account.')) {
                document.getElementById('clearAccountNumberForm').submit();
            }
        }
    </script>
}

@model ThriftLoop.DTOs.Admin.RejectRiderDto
@{
    ViewData["Title"] = "Reject Rider Application";
    Layout = "~/Views/Shared/_Layout.cshtml";
    var riderName = ViewBag.RiderName as string ?? "Applicant";
    var riderEmail = ViewBag.RiderEmail as string ?? "";
}

<div class="admin-approvals">
    <div class="admin-header">
        <div>
            <div class="admin-header__back">
                <a asp-action="RiderApplicationDetail" asp-route-id="@Model.RiderId" class="back-link">
                    <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true">
                        <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M17 10a.75.75 0 01-.75.75H5.612l4.158 3.96a.75.75 0 11-1.04 1.08l-5.5-5.25a.75.75 0 010-1.08l5.5-5.25a.75.75 0 111.04 1.08L5.612 9.25H16.25A.75.75 0 0117 10z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                    </svg>
                    Back to Application Details
                </a>
            </div>
            <h1>Reject Rider Application</h1>
            <p>Provide a reason for rejecting @riderName's application.</p>
        </div>
    </div>

    @if (TempData["ErrorMessage"] is string errMsg)
    {
        <div class="alert alert--error">@errMsg</div>
    }

    <div class="rejection-form-container" style="max-width: 600px; margin: 0 auto;">
        <div class="detail-card">
            <div class="detail-card__header">
                <h2>Application Summary</h2>
            </div>
            <div class="detail-card__body">
                <div class="detail-row">
                    <div class="detail-label">Applicant</div>
                    <div class="detail-value">@riderName</div>
                </div>
                <div class="detail-row">
                    <div class="detail-label">Email</div>
                    <div class="detail-value">@riderEmail</div>
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>

        <form method="post" asp-action="RejectRiderWithReason">
            @Html.AntiForgeryToken()
            <input type="hidden" asp-for="RiderId" />

            <div class="detail-card" style="margin-top: 1.5rem;">
                <div class="detail-card__header">
                    <h2>Rejection Reason</h2>
                </div>
                <div class="detail-card__body">
                    <div class="field">
                        <label asp-for="Reason" class="field__label" style="display: block; margin-bottom: 0.5rem; font-weight: 600;">
                            Please explain why this application is being rejected
                        </label>
                        <textarea asp-for="Reason" 
                                  class="field__input" 
                                  rows="5" 
                                  placeholder="e.g., Driver's license photo is blurry and unreadable.&#10;Vehicle registration information incomplete.&#10;Address verification failed."
                                  style="width: 100%; padding: 0.75rem; border: 1px solid #d1d5db; border-radius: 0.5rem; font-family: inherit;"></textarea>
                        <span asp-validation-for="Reason" class="field__error" style="color: #dc2626; font-size: 0.875rem; margin-top: 0.25rem; display: block;"></span>
                        <p class="field__hint" style="font-size: 0.75rem; color: #6b7280; margin-top: 0.5rem;">
                            This reason will be shown to the rider so they know what to fix.
                        </p>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>

            <div class="action-buttons" style="margin-top: 1.5rem; display: flex; gap: 1rem; justify-content: flex-end;">
                <a asp-action="RiderApplicationDetail" asp-route-id="@Model.RiderId" class="btn btn--secondary">Cancel</a>
                <button type="submit" class="btn btn--reject" onclick="return confirm('Are you sure you want to reject this rider application? The applicant will be notified and can resubmit with corrections.')">
                    Confirm Rejection
                </button>
            </div>
        </form>
    </div>
</div>

                    <input type="hidden" name="riderId" value="@Model.Id" />
                    <button type="submit" class="btn btn--approve" onclick="return confirm('Approve @Model.FullName as a rider? This will allow them to accept delivery jobs.')">
                        <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true">
                            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M16.704 4.153a.75.75 0 01.143 1.052l-8 10.5a.75.75 0 01-1.127.075l-4.5-4.5a.75.75 0 011.06-1.06l3.894 3.893 7.48-9.817a.75.75 0 011.05-.143z" clip-rule="evenodd" />

<script>
    // Click to enlarge license image
    document.querySelectorAll('.license-image').forEach(img => {
        img.addEventListener('click', function() {
            const modal = document.createElement('div');
            modal.style.position = 'fixed';
            modal.style.top = '0';
            modal.style.left = '0';
            modal.style.width = '100%';
            modal.style.height = '100%';
            modal.style.backgroundColor = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.9)';
            modal.style.zIndex = '9999';
            modal.style.display = 'flex';
            modal.style.alignItems = 'center';
            modal.style.justifyContent = 'center';
            modal.style.cursor = 'pointer';
            
            const enlargedImg = document.createElement('img');
            enlargedImg.src = this.src;
            enlargedImg.style.maxWidth = '90%';
            enlargedImg.style.maxHeight = '90%';
            enlargedImg.style.borderRadius = '0.5rem';
            
            modal.appendChild(enlargedImg);
            modal.addEventListener('click', () => modal.remove());
            document.body.appendChild(modal);
        });
    });
</script>

--- Views\Admin\RiderApprovals.cshtml ---
﻿<!-- Views/Admin/RiderApprovals.cshtml -->
@model IReadOnlyList<ThriftLoop.Models.Rider>
@{
    ViewData["Title"] = "Rider Approvals";
    Layout = "~/Views/Shared/_Layout.cshtml";
    var statusFilter = Context.Request.Query["status"].ToString();
}

<div class="admin-approvals">
    <div class="admin-header">
        <div>
            <h1>Rider Approvals</h1>
            <p>Review and process rider applications</p>
        </div>
    </div>

    <!-- Status Filters -->
    <div class="filter-tabs">
        <a asp-action="RiderApprovals" asp-route-status="" class="filter-tab @(string.IsNullOrEmpty(statusFilter) ? "active" : "")">All</a>
        <a asp-action="RiderApprovals" asp-route-status="pending" class="filter-tab @(statusFilter == "pending" ? "active" : "")">Pending</a>
        <a asp-action="RiderApprovals" asp-route-status="approved" class="filter-tab @(statusFilter == "approved" ? "active" : "")">Approved</a>
        <a asp-action="RiderApprovals" asp-route-status="rejected" class="filter-tab @(statusFilter == "rejected" ? "active" : "")">Rejected</a>
        <a asp-action="RiderApprovals" asp-route-status="resubmitted" class="filter-tab @(statusFilter == "resubmitted" ? "active" : "")">Resubmitted</a>
    </div>

    <!-- Riders Table -->
    <div class="table-container">
        <table class="admin-table">
            <thead>
                <tr>
                    <th>ID</th>
                    <th>Full Name</th>
                    <th>Email</th>
                    <th>Phone</th>
                    <th>Vehicle</th>
                    <th>Applied</th>
                    <th>Last Activity</th>
                    <th>Status</th>
                    <th>Actions</th>
                </tr>
            </thead>
            <tbody>
                @foreach (var rider in Model)
                {
                    // Determine status text and class
                    string statusText;
                    string statusClass;
                    bool isResubmitted = false;
                    
                    if (rider.IsApproved)
                    {
                        statusText = "Approved";
                        statusClass = "status-approved";
                    }
                    else if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(rider.RejectionReason))
                    {
                        if (rider.ResubmittedAt.HasValue)
                        {
                            statusText = "Resubmitted";
                            statusClass = "status-resubmitted";
                            isResubmitted = true;
                        }
                        else
                        {
                            statusText = "Rejected";
                            statusClass = "status-rejected";
                        }
                    }
                    else
                    {
                        statusText = "Pending";
                        statusClass = "status-pending";
                    }
                    
                    // Determine last activity date
                    DateTime? lastActivity = rider.ResubmittedAt ?? rider.RejectedAt ?? rider.UpdatedAt;
                    
                    <tr>
                        <td>@rider.Id</td>
                        <td>@(rider.FullName ?? "—")</td>
                        <td>@rider.Email</td>
                        <td>@(rider.PhoneNumber ?? "—")</td>
                        <td>@(rider.VehicleType ?? "—")</td>
                        <td>@rider.CreatedAt.ToString("yyyy-MM-dd")</td>
                        <td>
                            @if (lastActivity.HasValue)
                            {
                                <span title="Last activity: @lastActivity.Value.ToString("yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm")">
                                    @lastActivity.Value.ToString("yyyy-MM-dd")
                                    @if (isResubmitted)
                                    {
                                        <span class="resubmit-badge" title="Resubmitted">↻</span>
                                    }
                                    else if (rider.RejectedAt.HasValue && !isResubmitted)
                                    {
                                        <span class="rejected-badge" title="Rejected">✗</span>
                                    }
                                </span>
                            }
                            else
                            {
                                <span class="text-muted">—</span>
                            }
                         </td>
                        <td>
                            <div class="status-container">
                                <span class="status-badge @statusClass">@statusText</span>
                                @if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(rider.RejectionReason))
                                {
                                    <div class="rejection-tooltip" data-reason="@rider.RejectionReason">
                                        <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" width="14" height="14">
                                            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M18 10a8 8 0 11-16 0 8 8 0 0116 0zm-7-4a1 1 0 11-2 0 1 1 0 012 0zM9 9a1 1 0 000 2v3a1 1 0 001 1h1a1 1 0 100-2v-3a1 1 0 00-1-1H9z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                                        </svg>
                                    </div>
                                }
                            </div>
                         </td>
                        <td>
                            <div class="action-group">
                                <a asp-action="RiderApplicationDetail" asp-route-id="@rider.Id" class="action-btn btn-view">View Details</a>
                                
                                @if (!rider.IsApproved)
                                {
                                    <form method="post" asp-action="ApproveRider" class="inline-form">
                                        @Html.AntiForgeryToken()
                                        <input type="hidden" name="riderId" value="@rider.Id" />
                                        <button type="submit" class="action-btn btn-approve" onclick="return confirm('Approve rider @(rider.FullName ?? rider.Email)?')">Approve</button>
                                    </form>
                                    
                                    @if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(rider.RejectionReason))
                                    {
                                        <a asp-action="RejectRiderWithReason" asp-route-id="@rider.Id" class="action-btn btn-reject">Reject</a>
                                    }
                                    else
                                    {
                                        <a asp-action="RejectRiderWithReason" asp-route-id="@rider.Id" class="action-btn btn-reject">Re-Reject</a>
                                    }
                                }
                                else
                                {
                                    <span class="action-disabled">Approved</span>
                                }
                            </div>
                         </td>
                     </tr>
                }
            </tbody>
        </table>
    </div>

    @if (!Model.Any())
    {
        <div class="empty-state">
            <p>No rider applications found.</p>
        </div>
    }
</div>

<script>
    // Tooltip functionality for rejection reasons
    (function() {
        let activeTooltip = null;
        
        document.querySelectorAll('.rejection-tooltip').forEach(tooltip => {
            tooltip.addEventListener('mouseenter', function(e) {
                const reason = this.getAttribute('data-reason');
                if (!reason) return;
                
                // Remove any existing tooltip
                if (activeTooltip) activeTooltip.remove();
                
                // Create tooltip
                const tooltipDiv = document.createElement('div');
                tooltipDiv.className = 'rejection-custom-tooltip';
                tooltipDiv.innerHTML = `
                    <div class="tooltip-arrow"></div>
                    <div class="tooltip-content">${escapeHtml(reason)}</div>
                `;
                
                // Style the tooltip
                tooltipDiv.style.position = 'fixed';
                tooltipDiv.style.backgroundColor = '#1f2937';
                tooltipDiv.style.color = 'white';
                tooltipDiv.style.borderRadius = '0.5rem';
                tooltipDiv.style.fontSize = '0.75rem';
                tooltipDiv.style.maxWidth = '350px';
                tooltipDiv.style.zIndex = '10000';
                tooltipDiv.style.boxShadow = '0 4px 6px -1px rgba(0,0,0,0.1)';
                tooltipDiv.style.pointerEvents = 'none';
                
                const rect = this.getBoundingClientRect();
                tooltipDiv.style.bottom = (window.innerHeight - rect.top + 8) + 'px';
                tooltipDiv.style.left = rect.left + 'px';
                
                document.body.appendChild(tooltipDiv);
                activeTooltip = tooltipDiv;
            });
            
            tooltip.addEventListener('mouseleave', function() {
                if (activeTooltip) {
                    activeTooltip.remove();
                    activeTooltip = null;
                }
            });
        });
        
        // Helper function to escape HTML
        function escapeHtml(text) {
            const div = document.createElement('div');
            div.textContent = text;
            return div.innerHTML;
        }
        
        // Close tooltip on scroll
        window.addEventListener('scroll', function() {
            if (activeTooltip) {
                activeTooltip.remove();
                activeTooltip = null;
            }
        });
    })();
</script>

<style>
    /* Additional styles for custom tooltip */
    .rejection-custom-tooltip {
        position: fixed;
        background-color: #1f2937;
        color: white;
        border-radius: 0.5rem;
        font-size: 0.75rem;
        max-width: 350px;
        z-index: 10000;
        box-shadow: 0 4px 6px -1px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.1);
        pointer-events: none;
    }
    
    .rejection-custom-tooltip .tooltip-content {
        padding: 0.5rem 0.75rem;
        word-wrap: break-word;
        line-height: 1.4;
    }
    
    .rejection-custom-tooltip .tooltip-arrow {
        position: absolute;
        bottom: -6px;
        left: 12px;
        width: 12px;
        height: 6px;
        background-color: #1f2937;
        clip-path: polygon(0% 0%, 100% 0%, 50% 100%);
    }
</style>

@model ThriftLoop.ViewModels.Admin.TopUpReviewViewModel
@using ThriftLoop.Enums
@{
    ViewData["Title"] = "Top-Up Requests Review";
    Layout = "~/Views/Shared/_Layout.cshtml";
    const decimal priorityThreshold = 300m;
}

<div class="admin-topup-shell">
    <nav class="detail-breadcrumb" aria-label="Breadcrumb">
        <a asp-action="Index" asp-controller="Admin" class="detail-breadcrumb__link">
            <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.8">
                <path d="M12.5 5L7.5 10L12.5 15" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" />
            </svg>
            Back to Admin Dashboard
        </a>
    </nav>

    <div class="admin-topup-header">
        <div>
            <h1 class="admin-topup__title">Top-Up Requests Review</h1>
            <p class="admin-topup__subtitle">
                Review and approve GCash top-up requests.
                <span class="admin-priority-note">
                    ⚡ Transactions above ₱@(priorityThreshold.ToString("N0")) require manual approval.
                </span>
            </p>
        </div>
        <div class="admin-topup-stats">
            <div class="admin-stat-pill admin-stat-pill--pending">
                <span class="admin-stat__number">@Model.PendingCount</span>
                <span class="admin-stat__label">Pending</span>
            </div>
            <div class="admin-stat-pill admin-stat-pill--review">
                <span class="admin-stat__number">@Model.NeedsReviewCount</span>
                <span class="admin-stat__label">Needs Review</span>
            </div>
            @if (Model.HighValuePendingCount > 0)
            {
                <div class="admin-stat-pill admin-stat-pill--priority">
                    <span class="admin-stat__number">@Model.HighValuePendingCount</span>
                    <span class="admin-stat__label">High Value (>₱@(priorityThreshold.ToString("N0")))</span>
                </div>
            }
        </div>
    </div>

    @if (TempData["SuccessMessage"] is string successMsg)
    {
        <div class="admin-alert admin-alert--success" role="alert">@successMsg</div>
    }
    @if (TempData["ErrorMessage"] is string errorMsg)
    {
        <div class="admin-alert admin-alert--error" role="alert">@errorMsg</div>
    }

    <div class="admin-topup-filters">
        <span class="admin-filter-label">Filter:</span>
        <a asp-action="TopUpRequests" class="admin-filter-btn @(Model.CurrentFilter == null ? "admin-filter-btn--active" : "")">All</a>
        <a asp-action="TopUpRequests" asp-route-status="@TopUpStatus.Pending" class="admin-filter-btn @(Model.CurrentFilter == TopUpStatus.Pending ? "admin-filter-btn--active" : "")">Pending</a>
        <a asp-action="TopUpRequests" asp-route-status="@TopUpStatus.NeedsReview" class="admin-filter-btn @(Model.CurrentFilter == TopUpStatus.NeedsReview ? "admin-filter-btn--active" : "")">Needs Review</a>
        <a asp-action="TopUpRequests" asp-route-status="@TopUpStatus.Approved" class="admin-filter-btn @(Model.CurrentFilter == TopUpStatus.Approved ? "admin-filter-btn--active" : "")">Approved</a>
        <a asp-action="TopUpRequests" asp-route-status="@TopUpStatus.Rejected" class="admin-filter-btn @(Model.CurrentFilter == TopUpStatus.Rejected ? "admin-filter-btn--active" : "")">Rejected</a>
        <a asp-action="TopUpRequests" asp-route-status="@TopUpStatus.Voided" class="admin-filter-btn @(Model.CurrentFilter == TopUpStatus.Voided ? "admin-filter-btn--active" : "")">Voided</a>
    </div>

    @if (Model.Requests.Count == 0)
    {
        <div class="admin-topup-empty">
            <svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.5" width="48" height="48">
                <circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10"/>
                <path d="M12 6v6l4 2"/>
            </svg>
            <p>No top-up requests found.</p>
        </div>
    }
    else
    {
        <div class="admin-topup-table-wrapper">
            <table class="admin-topup-table">
                <thead>
                    <tr>
                        <th style="width: 30px;"></th>
                        <th>ID</th>
                        <th>User</th>
                        <th>Reference #</th>
                        <th>Amount</th>
                        <th>Account Match</th>
                        <th>Status</th>
                        <th>Submitted</th>
                        <th>Actions</th>
                    </tr>
                </thead>
                <tbody>
                    @foreach (var request in Model.Requests)
                    {
                        var isHighValue = request.Amount > priorityThreshold;
                        var isPriority = (request.Status == TopUpStatus.Pending || request.Status == TopUpStatus.NeedsReview) && isHighValue;
                        var rowClass = isPriority ? "admin-topup-row--priority" : "";
                        
                        <tr class="admin-topup-row admin-topup-row--@request.Status.ToString().ToLower() @rowClass">
                            <td class="admin-topup-priority-cell">
                                @if (isPriority)
                                {
                                    <span class="priority-indicator" title="High value - requires priority review">⚡</span>
                                }
                            </td>
                            <td data-label="ID">#@request.Id</td>
                            <td data-label="User">@(request.User?.Email ?? "Unknown")</td>
                            <td data-label="Reference #"><code>@request.ReferenceNumber</code></td>
                            <td data-label="Amount" class="admin-topup-amount @(isHighValue ? "admin-topup-amount--high" : "")">
                                ₱@request.Amount.ToString("N2")
                                @if (isHighValue)
                                {
                                    <span class="high-value-badge">High Value</span>
                                }
                            </td>
                            <td data-label="Account Match">
                                @if (request.AccountNumberMatched.HasValue)
                                {
                                    if (request.AccountNumberMatched.Value)
                                    {
                                        <span class="account-match account-match--yes">✓ Match</span>
                                    }
                                    else
                                    {
                                        <span class="account-match account-match--no" title="Receipt account number does not match expected GCash number">✗ Mismatch</span>
                                    }
                                }
                                else
                                {
                                    <span class="account-match account-match--unknown">—</span>
                                }
                            </td>
                             <td data-label="Status">
                                <span class="admin-status-badge admin-status-badge--@request.Status.ToString().ToLower()">
                                    @request.Status
                                    @if (request.IsAutoApproved)
                                    {
                                        <span class="admin-status-note">(auto)</span>
                                    }
                                </span>
                                @if (request.NeedsAdminReview)
                                {
                                    <span class="admin-review-flag" title="Needs admin review">🔍 Review</span>
                                }
                            </td>
                            <td data-label="Submitted">@request.CreatedAt.ToString("MMM dd, HH:mm")</td>
                            <td data-label="Actions">
                                <div class="admin-topup-actions">
                                    @if (request.ScreenshotPath != null)
                                    {
                                        <a href="@request.ScreenshotPath" target="_blank" class="admin-action-btn admin-action-btn--view">
                                            View Receipt
                                        </a>
                                    }

                                    @if (request.Status == TopUpStatus.Pending || request.Status == TopUpStatus.NeedsReview)
                                    {
                                        if (request.Amount > 0)
                                        {
                                            <form asp-action="ApproveTopUpRequest" method="post" class="admin-action-form">
                                                @Html.AntiForgeryToken()
                                                <input type="hidden" name="id" value="@request.Id" />
                                                <button type="submit" class="admin-action-btn admin-action-btn--approve" 
                                                        onclick="return confirm('Approve top-up of ₱@request.Amount.ToString("N2") for @(request.User?.Email)?')">
                                                    Approve
                                                </button>
                                            </form>
                                        }

                                        <button type="button" class="admin-action-btn admin-action-btn--review" 
                                                onclick="openReviewModal(@request.Id, '@request.ScreenshotPath?.Replace("\\", "\\\\")', @request.Amount, '@request.ReferenceNumber')">
                                            Review & Approve
                                        </button>

                                        <button type="button" class="admin-action-btn admin-action-btn--void" 
                                                onclick="openVoidModal(@request.Id, @request.Amount, '@(request.User?.Email)')">
                                            Void
                                        </button>
                                    }

                                    @if (request.Status == TopUpStatus.Voided && !string.IsNullOrEmpty(request.VoidReason))
                                    {
                                        <span class="admin-void-reason" title="@request.VoidReason">
                                            Voided: @request.VoidReason.Substring(0, Math.Min(30, request.VoidReason.Length))@(request.VoidReason.Length > 30 ? "..." : "")
                                        </span>
                                    }
                                    else if (request.Status == TopUpStatus.Rejected && !string.IsNullOrEmpty(request.RejectionReason))
                                    {
                                        <span class="admin-rejection-reason" title="@request.RejectionReason">
                                            Rejected: @request.RejectionReason.Substring(0, Math.Min(30, request.RejectionReason.Length))@(request.RejectionReason.Length > 30 ? "..." : "")
                                        </span>
                                    }
                                </div>
                            </td>
                        </tr>
                    }
                </tbody>
            </table>
        </div>

        @if (Model.TotalPages > 1)
        {
            <div class="admin-topup-pagination">
                @if (Model.CurrentPage > 1)
                {
                    <a asp-action="TopUpRequests" asp-route-page="@(Model.CurrentPage - 1)" asp-route-status="@Model.CurrentFilter" class="admin-pagination-btn">← Previous</a>
                }

                <span class="admin-pagination-info">Page @Model.CurrentPage of @Model.TotalPages</span>

                @if (Model.CurrentPage < Model.TotalPages)
                {
                    <a asp-action="TopUpRequests" asp-route-page="@(Model.CurrentPage + 1)" asp-route-status="@Model.CurrentFilter" class="admin-pagination-btn">Next →</a>
                }
            </div>
        }
    }
</div>

@section Scripts {
    <script>
        const PRIORITY_THRESHOLD = @priorityThreshold;
        let currentVoidRequestId = 0;
        let currentVoidAmount = 0;

        function openReviewModal(id, screenshotPath, currentAmount, currentRef) {
            document.getElementById('modalRequestId').value = id;
            document.getElementById('modalReceiptImage').src = screenshotPath || '';
            document.getElementById('modalAmount').value = currentAmount > 0 ? currentAmount : '';
            document.getElementById('modalReference').value = currentRef && currentRef !== 'MANUAL-REVIEW' ? currentRef : '';

            document.getElementById('reviewModal').style.display = 'block';
            document.body.style.overflow = 'hidden';

            var ocrDiv = document.getElementById('ocrScanning');
            if (currentAmount === 0 || currentRef === 'MANUAL-REVIEW') {
                ocrDiv.style.display = 'flex';
                setTimeout(function() {
                    ocrDiv.style.display = 'none';
                    if (!document.getElementById('modalAmount').value) {
                        document.getElementById('modalAmount').placeholder = 'Could not detect - enter manually';
                    }
                    if (!document.getElementById('modalReference').value) {
                        document.getElementById('modalReference').placeholder = 'Could not detect - enter manually';
                    }
                }, 1500);
            } else {
                ocrDiv.style.display = 'none';
            }
        }

        function closeReviewModal() {
            document.getElementById('reviewModal').style.display = 'none';
            document.body.style.overflow = '';
        }

        function openVoidModal(id, amount, userEmail) {
            currentVoidRequestId = id;
            currentVoidAmount = amount;
            
            const isHighValue = amount > PRIORITY_THRESHOLD;
            const infoDiv = document.getElementById('voidInfo');
            const warningDiv = document.getElementById('voidWarning');
            
            infoDiv.innerHTML = `
                <strong>Request #${id}</strong><br>
                User: ${userEmail || 'Unknown'}<br>
                Amount: ₱${amount.toLocaleString('en-PH', {minimumFractionDigits: 2})}
                ${isHighValue ? '<br><span style="color: #dc2626;">⚠️ High-value transaction</span>' : ''}
            `;
            
            if (isHighValue) {
                warningDiv.innerHTML = `
                    <strong>⚠️ High-Value Transaction</strong><br>
                    Voiding this transaction will indicate there might be an error with it. 
                    Please ensure you've verified all details before proceeding.
                `;
            } else {
                warningDiv.innerHTML = `
                    <strong>Note:</strong> Please provide a clear reason for voiding this transaction 
                    (e.g., duplicate transaction, invalid reference number, etc.).
                `;
            }
            
            document.getElementById('voidRequestId').value = id;
            document.getElementById('voidReasonSelect').value = '';
            document.getElementById('voidReasonText').value = '';
            document.getElementById('voidModal').style.display = 'block';
            document.body.style.overflow = 'hidden';
        }

        function closeVoidModal() {
            document.getElementById('voidModal').style.display = 'none';
            document.body.style.overflow = '';
        }

        function updateVoidReason() {
            const select = document.getElementById('voidReasonSelect');
            const textarea = document.getElementById('voidReasonText');
            const selectedReason = select.value;
            
            if (selectedReason && selectedReason !== 'Other') {
                textarea.value = selectedReason;
            } else if (selectedReason === 'Other') {
                textarea.value = '';
                textarea.focus();
            }
        }

        // Close modals on Escape key
        document.addEventListener('keydown', function(e) {
            if (e.key === 'Escape') {
                closeReviewModal();
                closeVoidModal();
            }
        });

        // Close modals when clicking outside content
        document.querySelectorAll('.admin-modal__overlay').forEach(overlay => {
            overlay.addEventListener('click', function() {
                closeReviewModal();
                closeVoidModal();
            });
        });
    </script>
}

                                <input type="hidden" name="isDisabled" value="@(!user.IsDisabled)" />
                                <button type="submit" 
                                        onclick="return confirm('@(user.IsDisabled ? "Enable" : "Disable") user @user.Email?')"
                                        style="padding: 6px 12px; border-radius: 6px; font-size: 0.75rem; font-weight: 600; border: none; cursor: pointer; transition: all 0.2s; background: @(user.IsDisabled ? "#ecfdf5" : "#fef2f2"); color: @(user.IsDisabled ? "#059669" : "#dc2626");"
                                        onmouseover="this.style.opacity='0.8'" onmouseout="this.style.opacity='1'">
                                    @(user.IsDisabled ? "Enable" : "Disable")
                                </button>
                            </form>
                        </td>
                    </tr>
                }
            </tbody>
        </table>
    </div>

    <!-- Pagination -->

    {

            {

                   class="admin-header__btn admin-header__btn--ghost" style="text-decoration: none;">← Previous</a>

            <span style="color: #6b7280; font-size: 0.9rem;">Page <strong style="color: #111827;">@Model.CurrentPage</strong> of <strong style="color: #111827;">@Model.TotalPages</strong></span>

            }
        </div>
    }
</div>

                                            onmouseover="this.style.opacity='0.8'" onmouseout="this.style.opacity='1'">Mark Completed</button>
                                </form>
                            }
                            else
                            {
                                <span style="color: #9ca3af; font-size: 0.9rem;">—</span>
                            }
                        </td>
                    </tr>
                }
            </tbody>
        </table>
    </div>

    @if (!Model.Any())
    {
        <div class="recent-card" style="text-align: center; padding: 60px;">
            <p style="color: #6b7280; font-size: 1rem;">No withdrawals found.</p>
        </div>
    }
</div>

<script>
    (function() {
        // Modal functionality for the search modal
        const modal = document.getElementById('userSearchModal');
        const searchInput = document.getElementById('userSearchInput');
        const clearBtn = document.getElementById('clearSearchBtn');
        const searchResults = document.getElementById('userSearchResults');
        const searchLoading = document.getElementById('searchLoading');
        const selectedUserId = document.getElementById('selectedUserId');
        const selectedUserDisplay = document.getElementById('selectedUserDisplay');
        const newMessageForm = document.getElementById('newMessageForm');
        const startChatBtn = document.getElementById('startChatBtn');
        const changeUserBtn = document.getElementById('changeUserBtn');
        const initialMessage = document.getElementById('initialMessage');
        const charCount = document.getElementById('charCount');
        
        let searchTimeout = null;
        let selectedUserData = null;
        
        // Character count for message
        if (initialMessage) {
            initialMessage.addEventListener('input', function() {
                const count = this.value.length;
                charCount.textContent = count;
            });
        }
        
        // Clear search
        if (clearBtn) {
            clearBtn.addEventListener('click', function() {
                searchInput.value = '';
                clearBtn.style.display = 'none';
                showEmptyState();
            });
        }
        
        // Search input
        if (searchInput) {
            searchInput.addEventListener('input', function() {
                const query = this.value.trim();
                clearBtn.style.display = query ? 'block' : 'none';
                
                if (searchTimeout) {
                    clearTimeout(searchTimeout);
                }
                
                if (query.length < 2) {
                    showEmptyState();
                    return;
                }
                
                searchTimeout = setTimeout(() => performSearch(query), 300);
            });
        }
        
        // Change user button
        if (changeUserBtn) {
            changeUserBtn.addEventListener('click', function() {
                newMessageForm.style.display = 'none';
                searchResults.style.display = 'block';
                searchInput.disabled = false;
                searchInput.focus();
            });
        }
        
        function showEmptyState() {
            searchResults.innerHTML = `
                <div class="search-empty-state">
                    <svg width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.5">
                        <circle cx="11" cy="11" r="8"/>
                        <path d="M21 21l-4.35-4.35"/>
                    </svg>
                    <p>Type at least 2 characters to search for users</p>
                </div>
            `;
        }
        
        async function performSearch(query) {
            searchLoading.style.display = 'flex';
            searchResults.innerHTML = '';
            
            try {
                const response = await fetch(`/Chat/SearchUsers?query=${encodeURIComponent(query)}`);
                const users = await response.json();
                
                searchLoading.style.display = 'none';
                
                if (users.length === 0) {
                    searchResults.innerHTML = `
                        <div class="search-empty-state">
                            <p>No users found</p>
                        </div>
                    `;
                    return;
                }
                
                renderSearchResults(users);
            } catch (error) {
                searchLoading.style.display = 'none';
                searchResults.innerHTML = `
                    <div class="search-empty-state">
                        <p>Error searching. Please try again.</p>
                    </div>
                `;
            }
        }
        
        function renderSearchResults(users) {
            const template = document.getElementById('userSearchResultTemplate').innerHTML;
            let html = '';
            
            users.forEach(user => {
                let itemHtml = template
                    .replace(/{{userId}}/g, user.id)
                    .replace(/{{userName}}/g, user.name)
                    .replace(/{{userEmail}}/g, user.email)
                    .replace(/{{conversationId}}/g, user.existingConversationId || '')
                    .replace(/{{avatarUrl}}/g, user.avatarUrl || '')
                    .replace(/{{initials}}/g, getInitials(user.name))
                    .replace(/{{#hasExistingConversation}}([\s\S]*?){{\/hasExistingConversation}}/g,
                        user.existingConversationId ? '$1' : '');
                
                html += itemHtml;
            });
            
            searchResults.innerHTML = html;
            
            // Add click handlers
            searchResults.querySelectorAll('.user-search-item').forEach(item => {
                item.addEventListener('click', function() {
                    selectUser({
                        id: this.dataset.userId,
                        name: this.dataset.userName,
                        email: this.dataset.userEmail,
                        conversationId: this.dataset.conversationId
                    });
                });
            });
        }
        
        function selectUser(user) {
            selectedUserData = user;
            selectedUserId.value = user.id;
            
            // Render selected user
            const template = document.getElementById('selectedUserTemplate').innerHTML;
            const html = template
                .replace(/{{userId}}/g, user.id)
                .replace(/{{userName}}/g, user.name)
                .replace(/{{userEmail}}/g, user.email)
                .replace(/{{avatarUrl}}/g, user.avatarUrl || '')
                .replace(/{{initials}}/g, getInitials(user.name));
            
            selectedUserDisplay.innerHTML = html;
            
            // Switch to message form
            searchResults.style.display = 'none';
            newMessageForm.style.display = 'block';
            searchInput.disabled = true;
            startChatBtn.disabled = false;
            
            initialMessage.focus();
        }
        
        function getInitials(name) {
            if (!name) return '?';
            const parts = name.split(' ').filter(p => p);
            if (parts.length >= 2) {
                return (parts[0][0] + parts[1][0]).toUpperCase();
            }
            return name.substring(0, 1).toUpperCase();
        }
        
        // If there's an existing conversation, redirect instead of showing form
        window.checkExistingConversation = function(userId, conversationId) {
            if (conversationId) {
                window.location.href = `/Chat/Conversation/${conversationId}`;
                return true;
            }
            return false;
        };
    })();
</script>

--- Views\Shared\_Navbar.cshtml ---
@using System.Security.Claims
@using ThriftLoop.Repositories.Interface
@using ThriftLoop.Services.Interface
@inject IShopRepository ShopRepo
@inject ICartRepository CartRepo
@inject IItemLikeRepository LikeRepo
@inject IChatService ChatService

@{
    var userEmail = User.FindFirst(ClaimTypes.Email)?.Value
                        ?? User.Identity?.Name
                        ?? string.Empty;
    var displayName = userEmail.Contains('@') ? userEmail.Split('@')[0] : userEmail;
    var currentPath = Context.Request.Path.Value ?? string.Empty;

    // Check if current user is a Rider
    var isRider = User.HasClaim(c => c.Type == "IsRider" && c.Value == "true");

    // Resolve live shop name for the navbar pill (only for Sellers)
    var shopLabel = "My Shop";

    // Get cart count, likes count, and unread message count for authenticated users
    int cartCount = 0;
    int likesCount = 0;
    int unreadMessageCount = 0;

    var rawId = User.FindFirst(ClaimTypes.NameIdentifier)?.Value;
    if (int.TryParse(rawId, out var navUserId))
    {
        if (!isRider && User.IsInRole("Seller"))
        {
            var shop = await ShopRepo.GetByUserIdAsync(navUserId);
            if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(shop?.ShopName))
                shopLabel = shop.ShopName;
        }

        if (User.Identity?.IsAuthenticated == true && !isRider)
        {
            cartCount = await CartRepo.GetCountByUserIdAsync(navUserId);
            var likes = await LikeRepo.GetByUserIdAsync(navUserId);
            likesCount = likes.Count;
            unreadMessageCount = await ChatService.GetTotalUnreadCountAsync(navUserId);
        }
    }
}

<nav class="tl-nav">
    <div class="tl-nav__inner">

        @* Logo - Redirects based on user type *@
        @if (isRider)
        {
            <a asp-controller="Rider" asp-action="Index" class="tl-nav__logo">
                <svg class="tl-nav__infinity" viewBox="0 0 512 512" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" aria-hidden="true">

<script>
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
        const dropdownToggle = document.getElementById('userDropdown');
        const dropdownMenu = document.getElementById('userDropdownMenu');

        if (dropdownToggle && dropdownMenu) {
            dropdownToggle.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                e.preventDefault();
                e.stopPropagation();
                const isExpanded = this.getAttribute('aria-expanded') === 'true';
                this.setAttribute('aria-expanded', !isExpanded);
                dropdownMenu.classList.toggle('show');
            });

            document.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                if (!dropdownToggle.contains(e.target) && !dropdownMenu.contains(e.target)) {
                    dropdownToggle.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'false');
                    dropdownMenu.classList.remove('show');
                }
            });
        }

        // Poll for unread message count updates
        function updateUnreadCount() {
            fetch('/Chat/UnreadCount')
                .then(response => response.json())
                .then(data => {
                    const badge = document.getElementById('chatUnreadBadge');
                    if (badge) {
                        if (data.unreadCount > 0) {
                            badge.textContent = data.unreadCount > 99 ? '99+' : data.unreadCount;
                            badge.style.display = 'flex';
                        } else {
                            badge.style.display = 'none';
                        }
                    }
                })
                .catch(() => {});
        }

        // Only poll if user is authenticated and not a rider
        @if (User.Identity?.IsAuthenticated == true && !isRider)
        {
                <text>
                    setInterval(updateUnreadCount, 30000); // Poll every 30 seconds
                </text>
        }
    });
</script>

--- Views\User\index.cshtml ---
﻿@model ThriftLoop.DTOs.User.UpdateProfileDTO
@using ThriftLoop.Enums
@{
    ViewData["Title"] = "My Profile";
    Layout = null;

    var profile = ViewBag.Profile as ThriftLoop.DTOs.User.UserProfileDTO;
    var sellerApp = ViewBag.SellerApplication as ThriftLoop.DTOs.User.SellerApplicationStatusDTO;

    @* ── Address field validation state ───────────────────────── *@
    var addrError = ViewData.ModelState.ContainsKey("Address")
                    && ViewData.ModelState["Address"]!.Errors.Count > 0;
    var addrErrorMsg = addrError
                       ? ViewData.ModelState["Address"]!.Errors[0].ErrorMessage

    <script>
        (function () {
            'use strict';

            var form = document.getElementById('addFundsForm');
            var btn = document.getElementById('addFundsBtn');
            var fileInput = document.getElementById('receiptImage');
            var previewContainer = document.getElementById('previewContainer');
            var previewImage = document.getElementById('previewImage');

            // Image preview
            if (fileInput) {
                fileInput.addEventListener('change', function () {
                    var file = this.files[0];
                    if (file) {
                        var reader = new FileReader();
                        reader.onload = function (e) {
                            previewImage.src = e.target.result;
                            previewContainer.style.display = 'block';
                        };
                        reader.readAsDataURL(file);
                    }
                });
            }

            // Form submit
            if (form && btn) {
                form.addEventListener('submit', function () {
                    btn.disabled = true;
                    btn.innerHTML = '<svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" width="16" height="16" class="animate-spin"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M10 2a.75.75 0 01.75.75v2.5a.75.75 0 01-1.5 0v-2.5A.75.75 0 0110 2zM5.5 10a.75.75 0 01.75-.75h2.5a.75.75 0 010 1.5h-2.5A.75.75 0 015.5 10zm7 0a.75.75 0 01.75-.75h2.5a.75.75 0 010 1.5h-2.5A.75.75 0 0112.5 10zM10 14.5a.75.75 0 01.75.75v2.5a.75.75 0 01-1.5 0v-2.5a.75.75 0 01.75-.75zM3.22 5.22a.75.75 0 011.06 0l1.77 1.77a.75.75 0 11-1.06 1.06L3.22 6.28a.75.75 0 010-1.06zm11.31 1.77l1.77-1.77a.75.75 0 111.06 1.06l-1.77 1.77a.75.75 0 11-1.06-1.06z" clip-rule="evenodd" /></svg> Processing…';
                });
            }
        }());
    </script>
}

@using ThriftLoop.Models
@using ThriftLoop.Enums
@{
    ViewData["Title"] = "My Wallet";

    // Check if current user is a rider (transactions use ToRiderId instead of ToUserId)
    var isRider = User.HasClaim(c => c.Type == "IsRider" && c.Value == "true");
}

<div class="wlt-shell">

        <div class="wlt-toast wlt-toast--success" id="wltToast" role="status">
            <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" width="18" height="18" aria-hidden="true">
                <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M10 18a8 8 0 100-16 8 8 0 000 16zm3.857-9.809a.75.75 0 00-1.214-.882l-3.483 4.79-1.88-1.88a.75.75 0 10-1.06 1.061l2.5 2.5a.75.75 0 001.137-.089l4-5.5z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
            </svg>
            @successMsg
        </div>
    }
    @if (TempData["ErrorMessage"] is string errMsg)
    {
        <div class="wlt-toast wlt-toast--error" id="wltToast" role="alert">
            <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" width="18" height="18" aria-hidden="true">
                <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M18 10a8 8 0 11-16 0 8 8 0 0116 0zm-8-5a.75.75 0 01.75.75v4.5a.75.75 0 01-1.5 0v-4.5A.75.75 0 0110 5zm0 10a1 1 0 100-2 1 1 0 000 2z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
            </svg>
            @errMsg
        </div>
    }

    @* ── Balance cards ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────── *@
    <div class="wlt-cards">

        <div class="wlt-card wlt-card--available">
            <div class="wlt-card__icon" aria-hidden="true">
                <svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.5">
                    <path stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" d="M2.25 18.75a60.07 60.07 0 0115.797 2.101c.727.198 1.453-.342 1.453-1.096V18.75M3.75 4.5v.75A.75.75 0 013 6h-.75m0 0v-.375c0-.621.504-1.125 1.125-1.125H20.25M2.25 6v9m18-10.5v.75c0 .414.336.75.75.75h.75m-1.5-1.5h.375c.621 0 1.125.504 1.125 1.125v9.75c0 .621-.504 1.125-1.125 1.125h-.375m1.5-1.5H21a.75.75 0 00-.75.75v.75m0 0H3.75m0 0h-.375a1.125 1.125 0 01-1.125-1.125V15m1.5 1.5v-.75A.75.75 0 003 15h-.75M15 10.5a3 3 0 11-6 0 3 3 0 016 0zm3 0h.008v.008H18V10.5zm-12 0h.008v.008H6V10.5z" />
                </svg>
            </div>
            <div class="wlt-card__body">
                <p class="wlt-card__label">Available Balance</p>
                <p class="wlt-card__amount">₱@Model.Balance.ToString("N2")</p>
                <p class="wlt-card__hint">Ready to spend or withdraw</p>
            </div>
        </div>

        <div class="wlt-card wlt-card--pending">
            <div class="wlt-card__icon" aria-hidden="true">
                <svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.5">
                    <path stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" d="M16.5 10.5V6.75a4.5 4.5 0 10-9 0v3.75m-.75 11.25h10.5a2.25 2.25 0 002.25-2.25v-6.75a2.25 2.25 0 00-2.25-2.25H6.75a2.25 2.25 0 00-2.25 2.25v6.75a2.25 2.25 0 002.25 2.25z" />
                </svg>
            </div>
            <div class="wlt-card__body">
                <p class="wlt-card__label">In Escrow</p>
                <p class="wlt-card__amount">₱@Model.PendingBalance.ToString("N2")</p>
                <p class="wlt-card__hint">Held for pending orders</p>
            </div>
        </div>

        <div class="wlt-card wlt-card--total">
            <div class="wlt-card__icon" aria-hidden="true">
                <svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.5">
                    <path stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" d="M3 13.125C3 12.504 3.504 12 4.125 12h2.25c.621 0 1.125.504 1.125 1.125v6.75C7.5 20.496 6.996 21 6.375 21h-2.25A1.125 1.125 0 013 19.875v-6.75zM9.75 8.625c0-.621.504-1.125 1.125-1.125h2.25c.621 0 1.125.504 1.125 1.125v11.25c0 .621-.504 1.125-1.125 1.125h-2.25a1.125 1.125 0 01-1.125-1.125V8.625zM16.5 4.125c0-.621.504-1.125 1.125-1.125h2.25C20.496 3 21 3.504 21 4.125v15.75c0 .621-.504 1.125-1.125 1.125h-2.25a1.125 1.125 0 01-1.125-1.125V4.125z" />
                </svg>
            </div>
            <div class="wlt-card__body">
                <p class="wlt-card__label">Total Balance</p>
                <p class="wlt-card__amount">₱@Model.TotalBalance.ToString("N2")</p>

    @* ── Two-column lower section ─────────────────────────────────────────────── *@
    <div class="wlt-lower">

        @* ── Transaction history ──────────────────────────────────────────── *@
        <section class="wlt-section" aria-label="Transaction history">
            <header class="wlt-section__header">
                <h2 class="wlt-section__title">Transaction History</h2>
                <span class="wlt-section__count">Last @Model.RecentTransactions.Count</span>
            </header>

            @if (!Model.RecentTransactions.Any())
            {
                <div class="wlt-empty">
                    <svg viewBox="0 0 48 48" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.3" aria-hidden="true">
                        <rect x="6" y="10" width="36" height="28" rx="4" />
                        <path d="M6 18h36M14 26h8M14 32h6" stroke-linecap="round" />
                    </svg>
                    <p>No transactions yet.</p>
                </div>
            }
            else
            {
                <div class="wlt-tx-list">
                    @foreach (var tx in Model.RecentTransactions)
                    {
                        // Determine if this transaction is a credit (money coming IN to the current user/rider)
                        bool isCredit;
                        
                        if (isRider)
                        {
                            // For riders: credit if ToRiderId matches current user
                            isCredit = tx.ToRiderId == Model.CurrentUserId
                                && tx.Type != TransactionType.EscrowHold
                                && tx.Type != TransactionType.Withdrawal;
                        }
                        else
                        {
                            // For regular users: credit if ToUserId matches current user
                            isCredit = tx.ToUserId == Model.CurrentUserId
                                && tx.Type != TransactionType.EscrowHold
                                && tx.Type != TransactionType.Withdrawal;
                        }
                        
                        bool isDebit = !isCredit;

                        string typeLabel = tx.Type switch
                        {
                            TransactionType.EscrowHold => "Escrow Hold",
                            TransactionType.EscrowRelease => "Escrow Release",
                            TransactionType.Withdrawal => "Withdrawal",
                            TransactionType.CashCollection => "Cash Collected",
                            TransactionType.TopUp => "Funds Added",
                            TransactionType.DeliveryFeePayment => "Delivery Fee",
                            _ => tx.Type.ToString()
                        };

                        string typeIcon = tx.Type switch
                        {
                            TransactionType.EscrowHold => "lock",
                            TransactionType.EscrowRelease => "unlock",
                            TransactionType.Withdrawal => "arrow-up",
                            TransactionType.CashCollection => "cash",
                            TransactionType.TopUp => "plus",
                            TransactionType.DeliveryFeePayment => "delivery",
                            _ => "dot"
                        };

                        <div class="wlt-tx @(isCredit ? "wlt-tx--credit" : "wlt-tx--debit")">
                            <div class="wlt-tx__icon wlt-tx__icon--@typeIcon" aria-hidden="true">
                                @if (typeIcon == "lock")
                                {
                                    <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" width="16" height="16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M10 1a4.5 4.5 0 00-4.5 4.5V9H5a2 2 0 00-2 2v6a2 2 0 002 2h10a2 2 0 002-2v-6a2 2 0 00-2-2h-.5V5.5A4.5 4.5 0 0010 1zm3 8V5.5a3 3 0 10-6 0V9h6z" clip-rule="evenodd" /></svg>
                                }
                                else if (typeIcon == "unlock")
                                {
                                    <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" width="16" height="16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M14.5 1A4.5 4.5 0 0010 5.5V9H3a2 2 0 00-2 2v6a2 2 0 002 2h10a2 2 0 002-2v-6a2 2 0 00-2-2h-1.5V5.5a3 3 0 116 0v2.75a.75.75 0 001.5 0V5.5A4.5 4.5 0 0014.5 1z" clip-rule="evenodd" /></svg>
                                }
                                else if (typeIcon == "arrow-up")
                                {
                                    <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" width="16" height="16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M10 17a.75.75 0 01-.75-.75V5.612L5.29 9.77a.75.75 0 01-1.08-1.04l5.25-5.5a.75.75 0 011.08 0l5.25 5.5a.75.75 0 11-1.08 1.04l-3.96-4.158V16.25A.75.75 0 0110 17z" clip-rule="evenodd" /></svg>
                                }
                                else if (typeIcon == "cash")
                                {
                                    <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" width="16" height="16"><path d="M10.75 10.818v2.614A3.13 3.13 0 0011.888 13c.482-.315.612-.648.612-.875 0-.227-.13-.56-.612-.875a3.13 3.13 0 00-1.138-.432zM8.33 8.62c.053.055.115.11.184.164.208.16.46.284.736.363V6.603a2.45 2.45 0 00-.35.13c-.14.065-.27.143-.386.233-.377.292-.514.627-.514.909 0 .184.058.39.33.585z" /><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M1 4a1 1 0 011-1h16a1 1 0 011 1v8a1 1 0 01-1 1H2a1 1 0 01-1-1V4zm2 3a2 2 0 00-2 2v1a2 2 0 002 2h.01A5.002 5.002 0 009.99 13H10a5 5 0 004.99-4.5H15a2 2 0 002-2V7a2 2 0 00-2-2v-.5a.5.5 0 00-1 0V5H6v-.5a.5.5 0 00-1 0V5H3z" clip-rule="evenodd" /></svg>
                                }
                                else if (typeIcon == "delivery")
                                {
                                    <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" width="16" height="16"><path d="M6.5 3c-1.051 0-2.093.04-3.125.117A1.49 1.49 0 002 4.607V10.5h9V4.606c0-.771-.59-1.43-1.375-1.489A41.568 41.568 0 006.5 3zM2 12v2.5A1.5 1.5 0 003.5 16h.041a3 3 0 005.918 0h.791a.75.75 0 00.75-.75V12H2z" /><path d="M6.5 18a1.5 1.5 0 100-3 1.5 1.5 0 000 3zM13.25 5.75a.75.75 0 00-1.5 0v2.5a.75.75 0 001.5 0v-2.5z" /><path d="M13 9.5a2.5 2.5 0 100-5 2.5 2.5 0 000 5z" /></svg>
                                }
                                else
                                {
                                    <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" width="16" height="16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M10 18a8 8 0 100-16 8 8 0 000 16zm3.857-9.809a.75.75 0 00-1.214-.882l-3.483 4.79-1.88-1.88a.75.75 0 10-1.06 1.061l2.5 2.5a.75.75 0 001.137-.089l4-5.5z" clip-rule="evenodd" /></svg>
                                }
                            </div>

                            <div class="wlt-tx__body">
                                <p class="wlt-tx__type">@typeLabel</p>
                                @if (tx.Order?.Item is not null)
                                {
                                    <p class="wlt-tx__ref">@tx.Order.Item.Title</p>
                                }
                                <p class="wlt-tx__date">
                                    <time datetime="@tx.CreatedAt.ToString("O")">
                                        @tx.CreatedAt.ToString("MMM d, yyyy · h:mm tt") UTC
                                    </time>
                                </p>
                            </div>

                            <div class="wlt-tx__amount @(isCredit ? "wlt-tx__amount--credit" : "wlt-tx__amount--debit")">
                                @(isCredit ? "+" : "−")₱@tx.Amount.ToString("N2")
                            </div>
                        </div>
                    }
                </div>
            }
        </section>

        @* ── Withdrawal history ───────────────────────────────────────────── *@
        <section class="wlt-section" aria-label="Withdrawal requests">
            <header class="wlt-section__header">
                <h2 class="wlt-section__title">Withdrawals</h2>
                <a asp-action="Withdraw" class="wlt-section__cta">Request payout →</a>
            </header>

            @if (!Model.Withdrawals.Any())
            {
                <div class="wlt-empty">
                    <svg viewBox="0 0 48 48" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.3" aria-hidden="true">
                        <path d="M24 10v28M14 20l10-10 10 10" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" />
                        <rect x="8" y="34" width="32" height="6" rx="2" />
                    </svg>
                    <p>No withdrawals yet.</p>
                </div>
            }
            else
            {
                <div class="wlt-wd-list">
                    @foreach (var wd in Model.Withdrawals)
                    {
                        string wdStatusClass = wd.Status switch
                        {
                            WithdrawalStatus.Requested => "wlt-badge--pending",
                            WithdrawalStatus.Processed => "wlt-badge--info",
                            WithdrawalStatus.Completed => "wlt-badge--success",
                            _ => ""
                        };

                        string wdMethodLabel = wd.Method switch
                        {
                            WithdrawalMethod.BankTransfer => "Bank Transfer",
                            WithdrawalMethod.PickupLocation => "Pickup",
                            _ => wd.Method.ToString()
                        };

                        <div class="wlt-wd">
                            <div class="wlt-wd__body">
                                <p class="wlt-wd__method">@wdMethodLabel</p>
                                @if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(wd.Reference))
                                {
                                    <p class="wlt-wd__ref">Ref: @wd.Reference</p>
                                }
                                <p class="wlt-wd__date">
                                    Requested
                                    <time datetime="@wd.RequestedAt.ToString("O")">
                                        @wd.RequestedAt.ToString("MMM d, yyyy")
                                    </time>
                                </p>
                            </div>
                            <div class="wlt-wd__right">
                                <p class="wlt-wd__amount">₱@wd.Amount.ToString("N2")</p>
                                <span class="wlt-badge @wdStatusClass">@wd.Status</span>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                    }
                </div>
            }
        </section>

    </div>

</div>

            font-size: 0.78rem;

        .wd-submit {
            width: 100%;
            justify-content: center;

    </style>

    <script>
        (function () {
            'use strict';

            var amountInput = document.getElementById('amountInput');
            var allBtn      = document.getElementById('withdrawAllBtn');
            var wdForm      = document.getElementById('wdForm');
            var wdSubmitBtn = document.getElementById('wdSubmitBtn');
            var methodRadios = document.querySelectorAll('.wd-method-radio');
            var methodLabels = document.querySelectorAll('.wd-method-option');

            // "Withdraw all" shortcut
            if (allBtn && amountInput) {
                allBtn.addEventListener('click', function () {
                    amountInput.value = amountInput.max;
                });
            }

            // Sync method option visual state with radio selection
            methodRadios.forEach(function (radio, i) {
                radio.addEventListener('change', function () {
                    methodLabels.forEach(function (lbl) { lbl.classList.remove('wd-method-option--active'); });
                    if (radio.checked) methodLabels[i].classList.add('wd-method-option--active');
                });
            });

            // Update reference hint based on method
            var referenceHint = document.getElementById('referenceHint');
            methodRadios.forEach(function (radio) {
                radio.addEventListener('change', function () {
                    if (!referenceHint) return;
                    referenceHint.textContent = radio.value === '1'
                        ? 'Your preferred pickup location or reference code.'
                        : 'Your bank account number or preferred pickup reference.';
                });
            });

            // Disable submit while in-flight
            if (wdForm && wdSubmitBtn) {
                wdForm.addEventListener('submit', function () {
                    wdSubmitBtn.disabled = true;
                    wdSubmitBtn.textContent = 'Submitting…';
                });
            }
        }());
    </script>
}
